match. Because of this wolf's intelligence, they have specific choices that lead them on to certain paths. <%= s.namePlayer %> can see a house in the distance... [[Approach the house->See 1st Pig]]As <%= s.namePlayer %> gets closer, they notice a small brittle house. It is slanted and severely unstable. <%= s.namePlayer %> knocks on the door and a small pig peeks out. He is wearing a beige straw hat with denim overalls. There is no way you paid for someone to build this.". The Little Pig's cheeks redden and they shout "Actually, I made this house by myself!". After glancing at the frail house again, <%= s.namePlayer %> replies "I'm not surprised in the slightest". The Little Pig pouts and closes the door. <% s.Aggressive = 5 %> [[Hold the door->Aggression2]] +Aggression <br> [["I'm sorry about that!"->FriendlyAgg]] +Friendliness <br> [["Hear me out"->ManipulationAgg]] +Manipulation"Sorry to disturb you" <%= s.namePlayer %> explains, "I've seemed to have lost my way and I cannot find my home. I'm <%= s.namePlayer %> by the way". The Little Pig peers at you but soon becomes composed once he takes in your demeanour. "I'm Ayo. Nice to meet 'cha" He gestures towards his abode "Come on in, I'll fix you a cuppa!" Gratefully, <%= s.namePlayer %> accepts Ayo's kindness and enters the small home. <% s.Friendly = 1 %> [[Enter house->Inside Small home]] +Friendliness <br> [[Eat Ayo->Aggression3]] + Aggression <br> [[Look at family photos->Manipulation3]] + Manipulation"You know, I wouldn't believe a small thing like you could make something so... wow." Ayo takes a step back "I don't think-" "I wouldn't normally" <%= s.namePlayer %> explains "But I'm really desperate" Ayo ushers you in. <% s.Manipulation = 10 %> [[Enter House->Manipulation4]] +Manipulation <br> [[Enter House->Inside Small home]] +Friendliness <br> [[Eat Ayo->Aggression3]] +Aggression<%= s.namePlayer %> stick's their foot at the entrance of the Little Pig's door and forces their way into the small home. The Little Pig screams "What-". Before he could finish what he was saying <%= s.namePlayer %> has swallowed the pig in one gulp. Without hesitation, <%= s.namePlayer %> then destroys the house, leaving not one piece of furniture in tact. <% s.Aggressive += 5 %> [[Look across the horizon->2nd Pig]]"I don't want you to take offence to what I've just said. "Again I'm really sorry about that" <%= s.namePlayer %> rambles, taking on a submissive demeanor, "I'll leave you to enjoy the rest of your day." <%= s.namePlayer %> turns around and runs away from the small house. <% s.Friendly = 1 %> [[Look across the horizon->2nd Pig]]<%= s.namePlayer %> obstructs the door before it closes. "You don't actually believe I was being serious... right?" The little pig throws <%= s.namePlayer %> a dirty look. "I'm helping you be aware of the deginerates of the world. You're easy to read which makes you a target" While the small pig takes the statement into consideration, <%= s.namePlayer %> scans the interior of the abode and spots a family of piggies. "That photo over there, who is-" <%= s.namePlayer %> is interrupted by the little pig blocking the entrance to his home. "Now listen ya big wolf!" The small pig puffs "I want you off my property right now" Sensing the pigs stubborness, <%= s.namePlayer %> cuts their losses and walks away from the lot. <% s.Manipulation = 10 %> [[Look across the horizon->2nd Pig]]<%= s.namePlayer %> approaches a clay house.
